## 9. Cycle 9.6 — 2026-05-01 13:08Z 33-min prod 502 → CLOSED via wrapper fix

**Window**: 2026-05-01 13:08Z–13:41Z UTC (21:08–21:41 TST). 33-min prod 502 outage during Cycle 9.5 closeout follow-up.

**Sequence**:
1. PR #55 `990e12a` merged 13:04Z → Deploy `25215298274` reported success but container failed to bind PORT.
2. 2 retry deploys `25215385484` + `25216075765` same 5b03348 sha — all GHA-success but prod stayed 502.
3. RCA root cause: 3 rapid-fire deploys all called `pnpm migrate` first; `pg_advisory_lock(9412, 20260413)` contention → migrate hung indefinitely → `pnpm start:api` never ran → container never bound PORT.
4. **Recovery**: Elva tagged `rollback-e88c641` at last green sha `e88c641`, dispatched workflow run `25216423003 --ref rollback-e88c641 --field service=api`. /health 200 at 13:41Z on deployment `880a89e8`.
5. **Forward fix (楊董 22:01 TST)**: `e098820 fix(api): start railway api even when migration stalls` adds `scripts/start-api-railway.mjs` wrapper — even if `pnpm migrate` hangs, `pnpm start:api` runs anyway. Deploy `25217229959` success 14:03Z. Prod GREEN restored on forward path.
6. **B 決策（楊董 22:30 TST）**: migrate.ts root-cause fix（lock_timeout/statement_timeout）defer to post-demo. Backlog #269 created.

**Files**:
- `evidence/cycle_9_6_rca/boot_repro_log.txt`
- `evidence/cycle_9_6_rca/bisect_table.md`
- `evidence/cycle_9_6_rca/green_fix_proposal.md`
- Memory: `feedback_no_local_artifact_excuse.md`（標記 GHA-conclusion-only verification 失敗 root case）

**New rule**: `feedback_demo_deploy_freeze_p0_only_2026_05_01.md` — 5/1 22:30 起到 5/4 09:00 demo，deploy 只允許 4 個 P0 觸發（prod down / data-loss / auth broken / security）；非 P0 全 backlog。
